# <a name="release-notes-for-semi-annual-channel-releases-in-2017"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-103">2017中半年通道版本的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-103">Release notes for Semi-Annual Channel releases in 2017</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8cfde-104">這些版本資訊會提供2017中的 Office 365 ProPlus 半年通道更新中所含之新功能、安全性更新和非安全性更新的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-104">These release notes provide information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus in 2017.</span></span> 
> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-105">下面也會提供 Visio Pro for Office 365 和 Project Online 桌面用戶端新功能、安全性更新和非安全性更新的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-105">The following also provides information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates for Visio Pro for Office 365 and Project Online Desktop Client.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-106">此資訊也適用於 Office 365 商務版，這是隨附一些 Office 365 方案 (例如，商務進階版) 的 Office 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-106">This information also applies to Office 365 Business, which is the version of Office that comes with some Office 365 plans, such as Business Premium.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-107">在 2018 年 1 月以前，半年通道的舊名為順延通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-107">Semi-Annual Channel was named Deferred Channel prior to January 2018.</span></span>

## <a name="version-1705-september-12"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-170">版本1705：9月12日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-170">Version 1705: September 12</span></span>

### <a name="access-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-172">Access：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-172">Access: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p101">**[新增功能] 對話方塊：** 在 Access 更新了新功能之後開啟 Access 時，會出現醒目提示新的 Access 功能對話方塊。您也可以使用 [檔案] \> [帳戶] \> [新增功能] 來開啟對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p101">**What’s New dialog:** A dialog box that highlights new Access features appears when Access is opened after Access is updated with new features. The dialog box is also available by going to File \> Account \> What’s New.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p102">**大型數字 (bigint) 支援︰** 使用 Access 表格中的大型數字資料類型來計算大型數字，並且連結至或從使用相同資料類型 (例如 SQL Server 中的 bigint) 的外部資料庫匯入。 [詳細資訊](https://blogs.office.com/2017/03/06/new-in-access-2016-large-number-bigint-support/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p102">**Large Number (bigint) support:** Use the Large Number data type in Access tables to calculate large numbers, and to link to or import from external databases that use an equivalent data type, such as bigint in SQL Server. [More information](https://blogs.office.com/2017/03/06/new-in-access-2016-large-number-bigint-support/)</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-177">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-177">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-178">**Windows 資訊保護（WIP）支援：**    Excel 現在是 enlightened 應用程式，而且可根據設定的原則，正確判斷要保護的公司與個人資料。  [詳細資訊](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-178">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:**   Excel is now an enlightened app, and can differentiate between corporate and personal data, correctly determining which to protect, based on configured policies.  [More information](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p103">**「取得與轉換」功能的改善︰** 在查詢編輯器中，藉由提供範例值來建立新資料行。隨著您鍵入，Excel 會偵測所需的轉換並顯示新資料行的預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p103">**Get & Transform improvement:** In the Query Editor, create a new column by providing sample values. As you type, Excel detects the required transformations and shows a preview of the new column.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p104">**插入最近的連結︰** 輕鬆地將超連結附加到最近使用的雲端型檔案或網站，並使用螢幕助讀程式為使用者建立有意義的顯示名稱。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p104">**Insert recent links:** Easily attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p105">**個人化預設樞紐分析表版面配置︰** 依您喜好的方式設定樞紐分析表，並在每次建立新的樞紐分析表時，以該版面配置開始作業。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/efd8569c-f07a-43c1-9db2-4f2912a0f94e)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p105">**Personalize the default PivotTable layout:** Set up a PivotTable the way you like, and start with that layout every time you create a new PivotTable. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/efd8569c-f07a-43c1-9db2-4f2912a0f94e)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p106">**取得與轉換功能的改善︰** 使用者可以依範例建立新的欄，並將表格欄分割成列。指定 SAP HANA 參數以及分組資料現在簡單許多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p106">**Get & Transform improvements:** Users can create new columns by example and split table columns into rows. Specifying parameters to SAP HANA and grouping data is now easier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-187">**增益集的集中式部署**系統管理員可以從 Office 365 系統管理中心部署並更新使用者或群組的增益集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-187">**Centralized deployment of add-ins**: Admins can deploy and update add-ins to users or groups from the Office 365 admin center.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8cfde-188">詳細資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-188">More information</span></span>](https://dev.office.com/docs/add-ins/publish/centralized-deployment)
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-189">**快速存取工具列自訂：** 下標和上標圖示可以新增至快速存取工具列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-189">**Quick Access Toolbar customization:** The Subscript and Superscript icons can be added to the Quick Access Toolbar.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-190">**取得與轉換功能的改善︰** 使用「查詢編輯器」分割資料行時自動偵測分隔符號字元，選擇要與合併二進位檔一起使用的範例檔案，並指定使用 DB2 連接器時要連線的封裝集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-190">**Get & Transform improvements:** Automatic detection of delimiter character when splitting columns using the Query Editor, choose which sample file to use with Combine Binaries, and specify the package collection to connect to when using the DB2 Connector.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p108">**杜拜字型：** 支援西歐語系以及使用阿拉伯文字集為主要語言的字型系列。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p108">**Dubai font:** Font family that supports both Western European languages as well as the major languages that use the Arabic script. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-193">**背景移除：** 使用任意格式的繪圖工具移除圖片背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-193">**Background removal:** Remove a picture background with a free-form drawing tool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-194">**取得與轉換功能的改善︰** 透過 ODCB 和 OLEDB 連接器使用 [導覽] 對話方塊中的「選取相關資料表」，直接從資料夾 [資料預覽] 對話方塊合併多個檔案，並且使用 [查詢編輯器] 視窗中的新內容功能表選項，在現有的查詢中插入新的步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-194">**Get & Transform improvements:** Use “Select Related Tables” in the Navigator dialog with the ODCB and OLEDB connectors, combine multiple files directly from the folder Data Preview dialog, and use a new context menu option in the Query Editor window to insert new steps in existing queries.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-195">**使用畫筆來選取及變更物件︰** 使用數位畫筆選取物件控點，來調整大小、旋轉、移動以及執行更多動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-195">**Use a pen to select and change objects:** Grab object handles with a digital pen to resize, rotate, move, and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p109">**地圖圖表：** 比較數值及顯示跨地理區域的類別。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p109">**Map Chart:** Compare values and show categories across geographic regions. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p110">**SVG 影像：** 插入並編輯活頁簿內的可縮放向量圖形 (SVG)。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p110">**SVG images:** Insert and edit scalable vector graphics (SVG) in workbooks. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-200">**插入圖示：**  移至插入\>插圖\>圖示，使用來自可縮放向量圖形（SVG）檔案的標準文件庫中的圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-200">**Insert icons:**  Use icons from a standard library of scalable vector graphics (SVG) files by going to Insert \> Illustrations \> Icons.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8cfde-201">詳細資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-201">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-202">**儲存至最近使用的資料夾︰** 在您移至 [檔案] \> [另存新檔] 時，使用 [最近] 索引標籤來儲存活頁簿至最近使用的資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-202">**Save to Recent folders:** Save a workbook to a recently used folder by using the Recent tab when you go to File \> Save As.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p112">**協助工具的改善：** 針對使用鍵盤、朗讀程式，以及其他輔助技術來讀取及編輯活頁簿的支援已獲改善。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/51fcb17a-b15b-4b13-ae04-d4f38ece3f78)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p112">**Accessibility improvements:** Improved support for using the keyboard, Narrator, and other assistive technology to read and edit workbooks. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/51fcb17a-b15b-4b13-ae04-d4f38ece3f78)</span></span>

### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-211">Excel：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-211">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-212">修正複製並貼上至 Excel 的問題，例如，忽略定位字元分隔 HTML 文字、不正確地移除空白資料列和資料行、忽略對齊方式，以及忽略公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-212">Fix issues with copying and pasting into Excel, such as ignoring tab-separated HTML text, incorrectly removing empty rows and columns, ignoring alignment, and ignoring formulas.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-213">修正此問題：當嘗試儲存與 OneDrive 用戶端同步的文件變更時出現錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-213">Fix an issue where errors appear when trying to save changes to documents synchronized with the OneDrive client.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-214">修正此問題：將工作表資料新增到資料模型中，且高對比佈景主題設定為黑色時 Excel 發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-214">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when adding worksheet data to a Data Model and the High Contrast theme is set to Black.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-215">修正此問題：包含外部連結的活頁簿導致 Excel 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-215">Fix an issue where Excel crashes for workbooks that contain external links.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-216">修正此問題：將儲存格從 Excel 貼到 Word 時，即使未選取「在具有零值的儲存格顯示零」設定，儲存格仍顯示為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-216">Fix an issue where pasting cells from Excel to Word shows zeros in the cells, even though the "Show a zero in cells that have zero value" setting is not selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-217">修正此問題：以程式設計方式套用建立於 Excel 2010 或更早版本中的活頁簿時，Excel 不會設定工作表保護密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-217">Fix an issue where Excel doesn't set the sheet protection password when applied programmatically for workbooks created in Excel 2010 or earlier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-218">修正此問題：在群組工作表中無法使用 [跨欄置中] 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-218">Fix an issue where Merge & Center doesn't work in grouped worksheets.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-219">修正此問題：遺失 Office 2016 版本之後所引入的新功能 (例如 TEXTJOIN、CONCAT、IFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-219">Fix an issue where new functions that were introduced after the release of Office 2016 - for example, TEXTJOIN, CONCAT, IFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS - are missing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-220">修正此問題：使用者嘗試套用儲存格層級權限時，發生 Excel 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-220">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when the user attempts to apply cell level permissions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-221">修正此問題：將大型檔案儲存到商務用 OneDrive 造成檔案鎖定，除非使用者關閉並重新開啟 Excel，否則無法編輯該檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-221">Fix an issue where saving a large file to OneDrive for Business causes the file to be locked and the user can't edit the file until the user closes and reopens Excel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-222">修正此問題：開啟 .xls 活頁簿時，新視窗會變成灰色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-222">Fix an issue where a new window appears grayed out when an .xls workbook is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-223">修正此問題：插入超連結時，Excel 可能會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-223">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when inserting hyperlinks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-224">修正此問題：新增 XML 對應時，Excel 可能會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-224">Fix an issue where Excel might fail when adding XML Maps.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-225">修正此問題：升級增益集之後，或從 Office 市集移除並再次下載增益集後，增益集的指令按鈕無法運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-225">Fix an issue where the command button for an Add-in doesn't work after the add-in is upgraded or after removing and downloading the Add-in again from the Office store.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-226">修正此問題：透過 VBA 處理 DLL 工作表時，Excel 可能會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-226">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when manipulating DLL sheets via VBA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-227">修正此問題：在圖表工作表上選擇表單控制項下拉式方塊時，Excel 會發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-227">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when selecting a form control combo box on a chart sheet.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p113">**Windows 資訊保護 (WIP) 支援：** OneNote 現在是已啟用的應用程式，而且可以區別公司與個人資料，根據設定的原則來正確判斷要保護的資料。 [詳細資訊](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p113">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:** OneNote is now an enlightened app, and can differentiate between corporate and personal data, correctly determining which to protect, based on configured policies. -   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-233">修正此問題：當畫面中有許多段落時，OneNote 畫布會隱藏內容或更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-233">Fix an issue where the OneNote canvas hides content or updates when many paragraphs are in view.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-234">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-234">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p114">**插入最近的連結︰** 將超連結附加到最近使用的雲端型檔案或網站，並使用螢幕助讀程式為使用者建立有意義的顯示名稱。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p114">**Insert recent links:** Attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p115">**杜拜字型：** 支援西歐語系以及使用阿拉伯文字集為主要語言的字型系列。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p115">**Dubai font:** Font family that supports both Western European languages as well as the major languages that use the Arabic script. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-240">**背景移除：** 使用任意格式的繪圖工具移除圖片背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-240">**Background removal:** Remove a picture background with a free-form drawing tool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-241">**檢查共用檔案的存取權︰** Outlook 會事先告訴使用者，收件者可能無法存取附加的 OneDrive 或 SharePoint 檔案，並建議如何修正這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-241">**Check access to shared files:** Outlook tells the user ahead of time if recipients may not be able to access an attached OneDrive or SharePoint file, and suggests how to fix the issue.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-242">**設定附件的權限：** 針對 OneDrive 或 SharePoint 的附件，使用者可以設定收件者不論在組織內部或外部，是否有讀取或編輯文件的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-242">**Set permissions on attachments:** For OneDrive or SharePoint attachments, the user can set whether recipients, in the organization or externally, have read or edit permissions to the attachment.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p116">**可釘選的工作窗格：** 在信箱中切換郵件時，讓增益集工作窗格保持開啟。 [詳細資訊](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/exchangedev/2017/01/26/pinnable-taskpane-in-outlook-2016/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p116">**Pinnable taskpane:** Leave the add-in taskpane open while switching between messages in a mailbox. [More information](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/exchangedev/2017/01/26/pinnable-taskpane-in-outlook-2016/)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p117">**SVG 影像：** 插入並編輯電子郵件內的可縮放向量圖形 (SVG)。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p117">**SVG images:** Insert and edit scalable vector graphics (SVG) in emails. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-247">**插入圖示：**  移至插入\>插圖\>圖示，使用來自可縮放向量圖形（SVG）檔案的標準文件庫中的圖示。  [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-247">**Insert icons:**  Use icons from a standard library of scalable vector graphics (SVG) files by going to Insert \> Illustrations \> Icons.  [More information](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-299">修正此問題：針對專案狀態日期之後所開始的工作，無法正確計算其 [實際完成百分比]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-299">Fix an issue where Physical % Complete doesn't roll up correctly for tasks starting after the project status date.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-300">修正此問題：成本與工時資源已指派給相同工作時，可能無法變更工作的狀態管理員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-300">Fix an issue when a cost and work resource is assigned to the same task, you may not be able to change the task's status manager.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-301">修正此問題：在某些專案中，撫平整個專案可能會陷入無限迴圈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-301">Fix an issue where for certain projects, leveling the entire project can leave you in an endless loop.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-302">修正此問題：有某些西班牙文的區域設定時，工作的開始和結束日期無法正確同步到 SharePoint 工作清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-302">Fix an issue where task start and finish dates don't synchronize to a SharePoint tasks list correctly if you have certain Spanish regional settings.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-303">修正此問題：從 Project 用戶端初始狀態核准程序時，可能永遠無法完成，而使專案停留在不穩定的狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-303">Fix an issue where if you initiate the status approvals process from the Project client, it may never finish, leaving the project in an unusable state.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-304">修正此問題：版面上同時有中文和英文字的情況下，預覽列印無法正確配置工作名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-304">Fix an issue where print preview doesn't layout task names correctly if you have Chinese and English words.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-305">修正此問題：將時間表以個別圖形複製到 PowerPoint 時沒有作用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-305">Fix an issue where copying the timeline into PowerPoint as individual shapes doesn't work.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-306">修正此問題：「專案間的連結」對話方塊意外顯示值「找不到檔案」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-306">Fix an issue where the "Links Between Projects" dialog unexpectedly displays the value "File Not Found."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-307">修正此問題：指派最大可用量為 0 的資源時，會產生不一致的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-307">Fix an issue you get inconsistent results when assigning resources with Max Units of 0.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-308">修正此問題：在刪除工作分派的開始日期時，將任務的開始日期重設為「越快越好」，忽略前置任務之類的內容，而導致工作分派的前置分割。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-308">Fix an issue where a task's start date gets reset to As Soon As Possible when deleting an assignment's start date, ignoring things like predecessors, which leads to leading splits on assignments.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p125">修正此問題：如果透過「最近」功能表從 SharePoint 開啟檔案，即使已啟用「是否要求在編輯文件前先取出文件?」設定，專案仍會自動簽出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p125">Fix an issue where if you open a file from SharePoint via the Recent menu, the project is automatically checked out to you even if the setting "Require documents to be checked out before they can be edited?" is enabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-311">修正此問題：如果直接進入「專案設定檔」應用程式，專案會發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-311">Fix an issue where if you go directly to the Project Profiles application, Project crashes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-312">修正此問題：對於從 Project 2013 進行升級的使用者，手動排定的任務無法正確更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-312">Fix an issue where manually scheduled tasks are not updated correctly for users upgrading from Project 2013.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-313">修正此問題：從 SharePoint 任務清單開啟專案時，專案可能會當機，因為專案開始任務同步處理程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-313">Fix an issue where when opening a project from a SharePoint task list, Project may crash as Project starts the task synchronization process.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-314">修正此問題：專案有時候會在建立小組時當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-314">Fix an issue where Project sometimes crashes when going to Build Team.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-315">修正此問題：儲存專案時基準資訊會遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-315">Fix an issue where baseline information is lost when saving a project.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-322">修正此問題：複製和貼上任務會攜帶基準資料並儲存資料，即便使用者不允許儲存受保護的基準資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-322">Fix an issue where copying and pasting tasks carries over the baseline data and the data is saved, even though the user isn't permitted to save protected baseline data.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-332">商務用 Skype：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-332">Skype for Business: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-333">**插入連結：** 將連結新增至 IM 與群組聊天中，並提供連結的易記文字而非完整的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-333">**Insert link:** Add a link into IM and group chats and provide friendly text for the link instead of the full URL.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p126">**共用畫面的通知：** 在 IM 交談中共用畫面時，或在您離開會議之後仍繼續共用畫面時，對話視窗中所顯示的通知。該通知會提醒您仍在共用畫面，並方便您藉由「停止共用」按鈕來停止共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p126">**Screen sharing notification:** A notification displays in the conversation window when you’re sharing a screen in an IM conversation or when screen sharing continues after you leave a meeting. The notification reminds you that you are still sharing your screen and makes it easy to stop sharing by using the “Stop Sharing” button.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-336">**Windows 資訊保護 (WIP) 支援：** 現在已支援商務用 Skype 作為「僅適用於 WIP (WIP Work Only)」應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-336">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:** Skype for Business is now supported as a WIP-work only app.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-337">透過在您允許的應用程式清單中加入 Skype，向 Windows 指示其不處理個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-337">  By adding Skype to your allowed apps list, it indicates to Windows that it does not handle personal data.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-338">Windows 會代表商務用 Skype 保護資料。  [詳細資訊](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-338">  Windows will protect data on behalf of Skype for Business.  [More information](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-339">**密碼重設選項：** 當使用者至少登入失敗一次時，登入視窗會顯示 [重設] 按鈕連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-339">**Password reset option:** A reset button link appears on the sign in window when a user fails to sign in at least once.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-348">商務用 Skype：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-348">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-349">修正此問題：加入會議且使用者看到音訊裝置加入對話方塊時，交談視窗沒有在背景顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-349">Fix an issue where a conversation window doesn't show up in the background when joining a meeting and the audio devices join dialog is shown to the user.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-350">修正此問題：Outlook 的會議連結不一定會傳遞正確的內部 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-350">Fix an issue where the meeting link from Outlook doesn't always pass internal URI properly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-351">擴大 [加入會議] 按鈕，以修正某些當地語系化語言的截斷問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-351">Widened the Meeting Join button to fix truncation of some localized languages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p128">變更了在原則停用音訊的情況下，嘗試呼叫使用者時所顯示的訊息，從「無法完成撥號」變更為「因為 IT 系統管理員已限制音訊而無法呼叫。請嘗試改用立即訊息或電子郵件，並要求洽詢 IT 系統管理員」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p128">Change message for attempted calls to users with audio disabled by policy from "Cannot complete the call" to "Cannot call because an IT administrator has restricted audio. Try using instant messaging or email instead and ask to check with their IT administrator."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-354">對已啟用 PSTN 會議的商務用 Skype® Online 使用者，在其會議邀請中新增了「忘記您的撥入 PIN」超連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-354">Add a "Forgot your dial-in PIN" hyperlink to meeting invites of PSTN Conferencing enabled users for Skype for Business Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-355">啟用從商務用 Skype® Online 加入 Teams 會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-355">Enable Teams meeting join from Skype for Business Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-356">將預設的喇叭工作階段音量從 40% 變更為 75%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-356">Change the default loudspeaker session volume from 40% to 75%.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-357">允許將索引標籤清單的最小寬度調整為較小的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-357">Allow resizing of the tab list to a smaller minimum width.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-358">更新了快速鍵以符合索引標籤的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-358">Update shortcut keys to match ordering of tabs.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-359">修正此問題：從行動裝置傳送時，希伯來文字的方向不正確。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-359">Fix incorrect direction of Hebrew text when sending from a mobile device.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-360">修正此問題：螢幕助讀程式朗讀 [展示桌面/授與控制權] 功能的資訊時所發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-360">Fix an issue with the information narrated by a screen reader for the Present Desktop/Give Control feature.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-361">在「選取聊天室」清單中，除了顯示已瀏覽過的聊天室之外，還顯示開啟的聊天室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-361">Show opened rooms in addition to followed rooms in Select Room lists.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-364">修正此問題：自動接受交談的交談視窗沒有最小化，反而開啟為一般視窗，而意外將焦點轉移至其他視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-364">Fix an issue that causes a conversation window for an automatically accepted conversation to open as a normal window, instead of minimized, and unexpectedly take focus away from other windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-365">修正此問題：在 [Skype 會議選項] 對話方塊中使用螢幕助讀程式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-365">Fix an issue with using a screen reader on the Skype Meeting Options dialog box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-366">修正此問題：邀請中的第一個訊息並未顯示在「未接的交談」電子郵件中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-366">Fix an issue where the first message in an invite isn't shown in the Missed Conversation email.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-367">修正此問題：在 Outlook 使用 [新增 Skype 會議] 按鈕建立會議邀請時，會顯示重複的撥打號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-367">Fix an issue where duplicate dial-in numbers are displayed when creating a meeting invite from Outlook using the New Skype Meeting button.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-368">修正此問題：垂直捲軸出現時，使用 Ctrl + A 全選時，不會選取 IM 記錄中的所有交談。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-368">Fix an issue where, when a scrollbar appears, all conversations in an IM history aren't selected when using Ctrl+A to select all.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-370">修正此問題：會議召集人使用「立即開會」與 3 位以上的參與者開會時，無法看到遠端參與者的視訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-370">Fix an issue where the meeting organizer is unable to see video of remote participants when using Meet Now with 3 or more participants.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-373">修正此問題：從 [諮詢轉接] 中的 IM 升級為音訊時，聊天區域無法關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-373">Fix an issue where the chat region does not close when escalating from IM to Audio in Consultative Transfer.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-376">為 [返回通話] 和 [轉接] 按鈕新增工具提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-376">Add tool tips for Back to Call and transfer buttons.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-377">請在 [諮詢轉接] 視窗中保留所花費的時間給螢幕助讀程式，例如 [朗讀程式]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-377">Make the time spent on hold in the consultative transfer window available to screen readers, such as Narrator.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-379">加入新的能力：進行諮詢的傳輸時，以滑鼠右鍵按一下 [傳輸] 按鈕可查看連絡人的電話號碼清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-379">Add the ability, when doing a consultative transfer, to right-click the "Transfer" button to see a list of phone numbers for the contact.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-488">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-488">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-489">**資料轉換與連線能力增強功能︰** 將清單展開到新的文字行，且值之間以分隔符號分隔，並在連線到 SQL 時指定容錯移轉選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-489">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** Expand a list into a new text column with delimiter between the values, and specify a failover option when connecting to SQL.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-490">**資料轉換與連線能力增強功能︰** 現在支援百分比資料類型，並增強二進位組合函數撰寫體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-490">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** The Percentage data type is now supported, and binary combining function authoring experiences have been enhanced.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-491">**OLEDB 連接器：** 使用 [取得及轉換] 中的新 [OLEDB 連接器]，透過指定連接字串 (或者要執行的 SQL 陳述式) 來建立查詢以匯入資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-491">**OLEDB connector:** Use the OLEDB connector in Get & Transform to create a query to import data by specifying a Connection String and, optionally, a SQL statement to execute.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p136">**筆跡重播：** 移至 [繪圖] \> [筆跡重播]，可往前和往後重播手寫來隱藏和顯示內容、提供逐步指示，或進一步了解他人想法的流程。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p136">**Ink replay:** Go to Draw \> Ink Replay to replay handwriting forward and backward to hide and reveal content, provide step-by-step instructions, or better understand the flow of others’ thoughts. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-494">**CSV (UTF-8) 支援︰** 開啟和儲存使用 UTF-8 字元編碼的 CSV 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-494">**CSV (UTF-8) support:** Open and save CSV files that use UTF-8 character encoding.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p138">**變更色彩：** 請使用 [操作說明搜尋] 來設定字型、醒目提示、圖形填滿等等。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/5bab7082-b772-427c-a106-14ae46f8687f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p138">**Change colors:** Use Tell Me to set the color for the font, highlighting, shape fill, and more. -   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p142">**與我共用的項目：** 移至 [檔案] \> [開啟] \> [與我共用的項目]，查看其他人與您共用的文件。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/e0476dc7-bf2f-4203-b9ad-c809578b03e7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p142">**Shared with Me:** See documents others have shared with you by going to File \> Open \> Shared with Me. -   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-622">[CVE-2017-8550](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/en-us/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-8550)：商務用 Skype 遠端程式碼執行弱點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-622">[CVE-2017-8550](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/en-us/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-8550): Skype for Business Remote Code Execution Vulnerability</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-623">商務用 Skype：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-623">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-624">修正此問題：自動接受交談的交談視窗沒有最小化，反而開啟為一般視窗，而意外將焦點轉移至其他視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-624">Fix an issue that causes a conversation window for an automatically accepted conversation to open as a normal window, instead of minimized, and unexpectedly take focus away from other windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-625">修正此問題：在公司網路內部和外部之間切換時，使用者無法登入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-625">Fix an issue where users are unable to sign in when switching between inside and outside corporate networks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-626">變更用來准許或拒絕參與者的大廳按鈕，從文字變更為影像 (X 或核取記號)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-626">Change the lobby buttons used to admit or deny participants from text to images (an X or a checkmark).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-627">變更會議提醒通知文字，從 [接受] 變更為 [加入]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-627">Change the meeting reminder notification text from "Accept" to "Join."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-628">更新收件者的狀態設為 [請勿打擾] 時，顯示給 IM 傳送者的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-628">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM when the recipient's status is set to Do Not Disturb.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-629">更新當收件者離線且 [儲存到歷程記錄] 停用時，顯示給 IM 傳送者的訊息，以讓其清楚知道收件者不會收到訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-629">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM, when the recipient is offline and "saving to history" is disabled, to make it clear that the recipient won't receive the message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-630">新增功能，以在群組聊天的聊天記錄和名冊之間移動垂直分隔列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-630">Add the capability to move the vertical splitter bar between the chat history and the roster in a group chat.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-631">新增功能，以調整 IM 或聊天室視窗中的索引標籤清單大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-631">Add the capability to resize the list of tabs in IM or chat room windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-632">新增功能，以在建立主題摘要時選取所搜尋到的聊天室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-632">Add the capability to select the chat rooms searched when creating a topic feed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-633">修正此問題：聊天記錄中間的交談不再出現訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-633">Fix an issue where message stop appearing in chat history mid-conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-634">修正此問題：交談視窗中出現重複訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-634">Fix an issue where duplicate messages appear in the conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-635">修正此問題：出現大量通知時，無法正確顯示快顯通知動作 ([接受] 和 [忽略])。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-635">Fix an issue where toast notification actions (Accept and Ignore) aren't properly displayed during a high volume of notifications.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-636">修正此問題：使用者在使用 Alt + Tab 開啟已最小化的交談視窗後無法輸入訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-636">Fix an issue where the user can't type a message after using Alt+Tab to open a minimized conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-637">修正此問題：即使 IM 可用，但使用者的連絡人卡片中，IM 按鈕仍會變為灰色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-637">Fix an issue where the IM button is grayed out in the contact card for a user, even though IM is available.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-638">修正此問題：多個交談視窗在關閉並重新開啟後並不會開啟回到其先前的大小和位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-638">Fix an issue where multiple conversation windows don't open back to their previous sizes and locations after being closed and reopened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-639">修正此問題：自訂連結在選取時不會啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-639">Fix an issue where custom links don't launch when selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-640">修正此問題：在 [區域] 欄位中的線上會議文字不會正確顯示非英文字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-640">Fix an issue where the online meeting text in the Region field isn't displayed correctly for non-English characters.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-641">修正此問題：在由右至左的語言中，通話持續時間等通知資訊不會正確呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-641">Fix an issue where notification information, such as call duration, aren't rendered correctly in right-to-left languages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-642">修正此問題：在建立主題摘要時，清除搜尋結果並不會將結果重設為已瀏覽過的聊天室清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-642">Fix an issue where, when creating a topic feed, clearing the search results doesn't reset the results to a list of followed rooms.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-643">修正此問題：同時開啟多個交談視窗時，商務用 Skype 發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-643">Fix an issue where Skype for Business hangs when multiple conversation windows are open at the same time.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-644">修正此問題：一旦關閉所有其他的索引標籤，最後一個對話視窗就會變成空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-644">Fix an issue where the last conversation window goes blank once all the other tabs are closed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-645">修正此問題：停用 [分頁對話] 之後，預設的焦點不在聊天輸入區域中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-645">Fix an issue where the default focus isn't in the chat input area when tabbed conversations are disabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p150">修正此問題：會議邀請中未出現「忘記您的撥入 PIN 嗎？」連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p150">Fix an issue where the "Forgot your dial-in PIN?" link doesn't appear in the meeting invite.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-648">修正此問題：在 [一般] 和 [音訊裝置] 頁面上，使用高 DPI 的螢幕而顯示比例為 175%或更高時，某些文字會遭到裁剪而截斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-648">Fix an issue where some text is clipped and truncated on the General and Audio device pages when using high DPI screens at 175% display or higher.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-649">修正此問題：當電腦是「永遠可用，永遠連線 (AOAC)」的電腦，若暫停電腦或在沒有網路的情況下繼續時，商務用 Skype 發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-649">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when the computer is suspended or resumed when there is no network and the computer is an "always on, always connected (AOAC)" computer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-650">修正此問題：使用 Polycom CX100 裝置通話時，未偵測到麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-650">Fix an issue where no microphone is detected in a call when using a Polycom CX100 device.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-651">修正此問題：在 IM 訊息中擇類似 \\\\servername 或 file:// 的連結時，會導致錯誤訊息而不會開啟位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-651">Fix an issue where choosing a link such as \\\\servername or file:// in an IM message results in an error message instead of opening the location.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-652">修正此問題：在使用位置型路由的虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 環境中，使用者無法進行或接收 PSTN 通話，因為伺服器認為使用者位置不是有效的 PSTN 通話位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-652">Fix an issue, in a Virtual Desktop Infrastructure (VDI) environment that uses location-based routing, where the user can't make or receive PSTN calls because the server thinks the location of the user isn't valid for PSTN calls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-653">使用者狀態設定為 [請勿打擾] 或 [正在進行簡報] 時，將針對未接訊息而傳送的電子郵件主旨列，從「來自 \<name\> 的未接交談」變更為「\<Name\> 已在商務用 Skype 中傳送訊息給您。」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-653">Change the subject line of the email sent for a missed message, when the user's status is set to Do Not Disturb or Presenting, from "Missed conversation with \<name\>" to "\<Name\> sent you a message in Skype for Business."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-654">開始擷取裝置上第一次登入的時間戳記，做為 [普查資料的一部分，](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/legal-and-regulatory/data-collection-practices) 以協助識別登入可靠性的趨勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-654">Start capturing the timestamp for the first time sign-in on the device as part of [census data](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/legal-and-regulatory/data-collection-practices) to help identify sign-in reliability trends.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-655">修正此問題：在 Window 10 版本 1607 (也稱為「年度更新版」) 上，共用次要監視器的選項沒有在特定監視器設定中出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-655">Fix an issue where the option to share a secondary monitor doesn't appear with certain monitor configurations on Window 10 Version 1607 (also known as the Anniversary Update).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-656">修正此問題：當共用者使用 RDP 的協力廠商實作並聚焦至共用內容時，商務用 Skype 發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-656">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when zooming into shared content when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-657">修正此問題：在虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 環境內，當使用者在進行語音通話時按一下 [音訊控制項]面板但並未出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-657">Fix an issue where the Audio Controls panel doesn't appear when a user clicks on the controls button in an audio call in a Virtual Desktop Infrastructure (VDI) environment.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-658">修正此問題：在使用者執行 Windows 7 時，首先共用了主要顯示器，接著切換為共用第二個顯示器，而檢視者看到黑色畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-658">Fix an issue where viewers see a black screen when a user is running Windows 7 and shares the main monitor first, and then switches to share a second monitor.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p151">修正此問題：在搜尋輸入方塊或「今日新鮮事？」區段方塊中，無法輸入特定符號 (例如：& 符號)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p151">Fix an issue where certain special characters, such as the ampersand (&), can't be entered in the search input box or the "What's happening today?" section box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-661">修正此問題：當有未讀離線 IM 時，未讀計數不會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-661">Fix an issue where the unread count isn't shown when there are missed offline IMs.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-662">修正此問題：「以電子郵件邀請」範本提及了 Lync，而非 Skype。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-662">Fix an issue where "Invite by email" templates mentioned Lync instead of Skype.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-663">修正此問題：在撥號鍵台下方的「我的號碼」區域內，缺少 LINE 號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-663">Fix an issue where the line number is missing from the "My Number" area below the dial pad.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-664">修正此問題：在聊天過程中，傳送訊息後滑鼠指標不會在 IM 輸入區域中顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-664">Fix an issue where the mouse pointer isn't shown in the IM input area after sending a message in a chat.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-665">修正此問題：在登入商務用 Skype 時，當載入快取集區發生問題的時候，出現當機情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-665">Fix an issue where Skype for Business hangs when signing in and there is a problem loading the cache pool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-666">修正此問題：在登入商務用 Skype 並還原交談時當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-666">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when signing in and restoring conversations.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-667">修正此問題：在恢復後，登入商務用 Skype 時當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-667">Fix an issue where Skype for Business hangs when signing in after resuming.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-668">修正此問題：在雙方組織內的 Exchange Server 皆已停用 TNEF 的情況下，會議連結遭到停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-668">Fix an issue where the meeting link is disabled if the Exchange servers in both organizations have TNEF disabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-669">修正此問題：若僅有一個進行中的 IM 交談，視訊通話無法重新啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-669">Fix an issue where a video call can't be restarted if there is only one IM conversation going on.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-670">修正此問題：將白板內容儲存為 PNG 檔案時，白板上的文字注釋會消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-670">Fix an issue where text annotations on a whiteboard are lost when saving the whiteboard as an PNG file.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-671">修正此問題：在 IM 視窗中輸入兩行以上的日文字時，第一行會消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-671">Fix an issue where the first line is hidden when inputting over two lines in Japanese in the IM window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-672">修正此問題：名稱中的 & 符號字元會錯誤地由底線字元所取代。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-672">Fix an issue where the ampersand character (&) is incorrectly replaced by an underscore character in names.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-673">修正此問題：在已排程會議中的「加入線上會議」URL 所發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-673">Fix an issue with the "Join online meeting" URL in a scheduled meeting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-674">修正此問題：即使已在作業系統內設定「將滑鼠暫留在視窗上方以啟動視窗」，仍然無法啟動視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-674">Fix an issue where hovering the mouse over a window doesn't activate the window even though the operating system is configured to do that.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-675">修正此問題：撥出電話交談歷程記錄項目中，顯示了來電者而非受話者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-675">Fix an issue where outgoing call conversation history items shows the caller instead of the called party.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-676">修正此問題：按 F12 時無法將交談儲存在本機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-676">Fix an issue where the F12 doesn't locally save a conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-677">修正此問題：遺漏的交談電子郵件並未包含初始 IM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-677">Fix an issue where a missed conversation email doesn't contain the initial IM.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-678">修正此問題：即使簡報者已停用 IM 參與功能，仍可在 IM 文字區域新增 Emoji。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-678">Fix an issue where an emoji can be added in the IM text area even if the presenter has disabled IM participation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-679">修正此問題：[鈴聲] 和 [聲音選項] 對話方塊的版面配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-679">Fix an issue with the layout of the Ringtones and Sounds option dialog box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-680">修正此問題：在關閉交談視窗時，商務用 Skype 發生當機情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-680">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when closing a conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-681">修正此問題：當網域註冊為虛名網域時，無 DNS 的登入會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-681">Fix an issue where DNS-less sign in fails when the domain is registered as a vanity domain.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-682">修正此問題：不會正確地儲存/載入常設聊天室通知設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-682">Fix an issue where persistent chat notification settings aren't being saved or loaded correctly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-683">修正此問題：即使已設置重新開啟交談的設定，在登入後，現有的端對端交談視窗或聊天室不會出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-683">Fix an issue where existing peer-to-peer conversation windows or chat rooms aren't showing up after signing in even though the setting to reopen conversations is set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-684">修正此問題：將作用中的交談靜音或取消靜音時，若其他交談視窗有未讀訊息，會使這些視窗顯示於畫面中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-684">Fix an issue where muting or unmuting the active conversation causes other conversation windows to appear as if they have unread messages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-685">修正此問題：已設定為略過媒體的使用者，在保留通話之後，無法透過 PSTN 閘道繼續通話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-685">Fix an issue where users that are configured for media bypass are unable to resume a call from a PSTN gateway after they put that call on hold.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-686">修正此問題：在使用協力廠商的 RDP 實作時，當使用者透過 URL 加入會議時，會看到藍色方塊而不是影像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-686">Fix an issue where the user sees a blue box instead of the video when joining a meeting via a URL when using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-687">修正此問題：SIP 位址的使用者部份會顯示，而非顯示快顯警示中的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-687">Fix an issue where the user part of the SIP address is showing instead of the display name in a toast alert.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p152">修正此問題：當商務用 Skype 透過連接埠 443 與 SIP 伺服器連線，且 Proxy 伺服器已存在時，如果 Proxy 不允許這些連線，則登入程序中會發生嚴重的延遲。透過在 HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync 下新增 EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 登錄項目，並將值設為 1，可啟用修正程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p152">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections. The fix is enabled by adding the EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD registry entry under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync, and setting the value to 1.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-690">修正此問題：如果使用分頁對話，在分頁上連按兩下並開始輸入文字時，有時候可能會造成焦點移至不同的分頁，然後繼續在該對話視窗中輸入文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-690">Fix an issue where, when using tabbed conversations, double-clicking on a tab and starting to type can sometimes cause the focus to move to a different tab and continue the typing in that conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-691">修正此問題：使用鍵盤時，無法在聊天記錄視窗中選取立即訊息中所包含的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-691">Fix an issue where URLs included in an instant message can't be selected in the chat history window by using the keyboard.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-692">修正此問題：如果選取 [鈴聲] 和 [音效] 選項下方的 [檢視 IM 交談及有人正在輸入時播放音效] 核取方塊，應該會聽到輸入音效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-692">Fix an issue where a typing sound should be heard if the "Play a sound when viewing an IM conversation and someone is typing" check box is selected under Ringtone and Sounds options.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-693">修正此問題：使用螢幕助讀程式 (例如 [朗讀程式]) 時，未宣告出現的對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-693">Fix an issue where dialog boxes that appear aren't announced when using a screen reader, such as Narrator.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-694">修正此問題：初次執行教學課程無法使用鍵盤進行瀏覽，而且螢幕助讀程式 (例如 [朗讀程式]) 無法進行讀取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-694">Fix an issue where the first run tutorial can't be navigated with a keyboard and can't be read by a screen reader, such as Narrator.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-695">修正此問題：在 [高 DPI] 設定中，工作列顯示狀態圖示未調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-695">Fix an issue where the taskbar presence icon doesn't scale in High DPI settings.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-696">修正此問題：無法使用鍵盤選取搜尋方塊中的清除欄位按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-696">Fix an issue where the clear field button in the search box can't be selected by using the keyboard.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-697">修正此問題：如果邀請來自另一個集區中的使用者，使用者無法啟動會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-697">Fix an issue where a user can't launch a meeting if the invite is from a user in another pool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-698">修正此問題：將自己新增至會議的使用者錯誤地顯示為不同的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-698">Fix an issue where a user adding themselves to a meeting is incorrectly shown as a different user.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-699">修正此問題：老闆來電時，狀態變更通知上的連絡人顯示狀態圖示遭到隱藏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-699">Fix an issue where the contact presence icon on the status change notification was hidden for incoming calls for the boss.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-700">修正此問題：IM 視窗中的文字游標閃爍率不符合 Windows 中的鍵盤內容設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-700">Fix an issue where the text cursor blink rate in the IM window doesn't match the keyboard properties setting in Windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-701">修正此問題：螢幕助讀程式宣告群組交談中不正確的連絡人名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-701">Fix an issue where a screen reader announces an incorrect contact name for a group conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-702">修正此問題：使用者無法使用鍵盤選取多位連絡人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-702">Fix an issue where user can't select multiple contacts by using the keyboard.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-703">修正此問題：無法從 Exchange 擷取使用者相片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-703">Fix an issue where user photos can't be retrieved from Exchange.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-704">修正此問題：使用者使用直接存取進行連線時，商務用 Skype 用戶端會連線到內部網路上的商務用 Skype Server，而不是外部網路上的商務用 Skype Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-704">Fix an issue where the Skype for Business client connects to a Skype for Business Server on the internal network, instead of one on the external network, when the user connects by using Direct Access.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-705">修正此問題：商務用 Skype 用戶端在嘗試解析會議擁有人的名稱時當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-705">Fix an issue where Skype for Business client crashes when trying to resolve the name of the meeting owner.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-706">修正此問題：在啟動或關閉商務用 Skype 時變更 Windows 設定，導致商務用 Skype 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-706">Fix an issue where changing a Windows setting while Skype for Business is starting up or shutting down causes Skype for Business to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-707">修正此問題：在常設聊天室中開啟參與者清單並嘗試將鍵盤焦點移到參與者清單時，商務用 Skype 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-707">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when opening the participant list in a persistent chat room and trying to move the keyboard focus to the participant list.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-708">修正此問題：商務用 Skype 在沒有網路可用的狀態下恢復執行時發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-708">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes on resume when no network is available.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-754">Office 套件：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-754">Office suite: Non-security updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-757">修正此問題：使用滑鼠並以筆跡繪圖時，放開滑鼠按鈕時會導致筆跡稍微偏移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-757">Fix an issue where, when drawing with ink and using a mouse, releasing the mouse button causes the ink to shift slightly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-758">修正此問題：在 Office 文件中插入 SVG 影像後，SVG 影像會在儲存和重新開啟文件時消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-758">Fix an issue where, after inserting an SVG image in an Office document, the SVG image disappears when the document is saved and re-opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-759">修正此問題：非英文版使用者在啟動 Office 期間，顯示下列錯誤訊息：「產品金鑰的最大長度為 25 個字元。」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-759">Fix an issue where Office shows the following error message during activation for non-English users: "The maximum length of the product key is 25 characters."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-760">修正此問題：VBA 表單造成框架圖層順序停止運作或顯示不正常的情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-760">Fix an issue with VBA forms that can cause the z-order of frames to stop functioning or display incorrectly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-761">修正此問題：由 Configuration Manager 的更新 trigged 將登錄中的 UpdateChannel 設定變更為不是有效更新通道的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-761">Fix an issue where an update trigged by Configuration Manager changes the UpdateChannel setting in the registry to something that's not a valid update channel.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-847">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-847">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-848">**資料轉換與連線能力增強功能︰** 將參數新增至查詢、從合併或附加作業建立新查詢，以及使用 Web 連接器來預覽網頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-848">**Data Transformation and Connectivity enhancements:** Add parameters to queries, create new queries from Merge or Append operations, and use the Web connector to preview web pages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-849">**圖表的巨集錄製︰** 支援樹狀圖、長條圖、柏拉圖、瀑布圖及盒鬚圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-849">**Macro recording for charts:** Support for Treemap, Histogram, Pareto, Waterfall, and Box & Whisker charts.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-850">**保留的 Power Query 版面配置：** 重新整理查詢後，使用「取得並轉換」匯入的資料格式和計算的欄會加以保留。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-850">**Power Query layouts preserved:** Formats and calculated columns for data imported using Get & Transform are preserved after queries refresh.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-851">**資料轉換與連線能力改進︰** 執行其他日期/時間轉換和文字操作、將活頁簿移轉到不同的環境、群組兩個以上的子句以進行資料列篩選，以及在 [查詢編輯器] 視窗中轉換文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-851">**Data transformation and connectivity improvements:** Perform additional Date/Time transformation and Text manipulations, migrate workbooks to a different environment, group two or more clauses for row filtering, and document transformations within the Query Editor window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-852">**發佈到 Power BI：** 透過 Power BI 訂閱將本機儲存的檔案發佈到 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-852">**Publish to Power BI:** Publish locally stored files to Power BI, with a Power BI subscription.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-853">**圖形辨識︰** 自動將繪圖轉換成圖形。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-853">**Shape Recognition:** Automatically transform your drawings into shapes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-854">**新增連接器：** 使用新的 Online Services 類別選項來建立查詢，包括 SharePoint Online、Exchange 和 SAP HANA 的連接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-854">**New connectors:** Create a query using options from the new Online Services category including connectors to SharePoint Online, Exchange, and SAP HANA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-855">**OLAP 連線與樞紐分析表︰** 改進以 OLAP 連線來建立、編輯和重新整理樞紐分析表時的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-855">**PivotTables with OLAP connections:** Improved the performance when you create, edit, and refresh PivotTables with OLAP connections.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-856">**資料轉換功能改良：** 將持續時間值轉換為年、支援在 [查詢編輯器] 預覽中的空白字元和換行字元，以及直接從 [查詢] 窗格重新命名查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-856">**Data transformation improvements:** Convert duration values to years, support for whitespace and line feeds in Query Editor preview, and rename queries directly from the Queries pane.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-857">**資料連線功能改良：** 偵測不規則的 CSV 檔案、支援使用 Exchange 連接器驗證 Microsoft 帳戶，以及驗證使用者嘗試連線到 SharePoint 清單時所提供的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-857">**Data connectivity improvements:** Detect jagged CSV files, support for authentication with a Microsoft account when using the Exchange connector, and validate URLs provided by users when trying to connect to their SharePoint List.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-863">Excel：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-863">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-864">修正此問題：使用 [編輯量值] 對話方塊會造成 Excel 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-864">Fix an issue where using an Edit Measure dialog box causes Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-865">修正此問題：使用 VBA 程式碼複製工作表時會使隱藏的工作表取消隱藏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-865">Fix an issue where using VBA code to copy a worksheet unhides worksheets that are hidden.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-866">修正此問題：使用規劃求解時，在選擇 [求解] 之後出現「找不到檔案 Solver32.dll」錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-866">Fix an issue where, when using Solver, a "File not found Solver32.dll" error message appears after choosing Solve.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-867">修正此問題：使用「高 DPI」監視器並啟用功能區的觸控模式時，未出現 Bing 地圖增益集的圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-867">Fix an issue where the icon for the Bing Map Add-in doesn't appear when using a High DPI monitor and touch mode is enabled for the ribbon.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-868">修正此問題：條件式格式化規則在開啟以 .xls 格式儲存的檔案之後無法運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-868">Fix an issue where conditional formatting rules don't work after opening a file that's been saved in the .xls format.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-869">修正 64 位元版本的 Excel 問題：當使用者嘗試連接 Access 查詢，且查詢參考連結的 ODBC 資料表時，使用者得到錯誤結果，而不是密碼提示 (其需要密碼提示才能向後端伺服器進行驗證)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-869">Fix an issue with the 64-bit version of Excel where the user gets an error, instead of a password prompt, when trying to connect to Access queries that reference linked ODBC tables that require a password prompt for authentication to the back-end server.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-870">修正此問題：從下拉式清單中選擇項目時，Excel 會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-870">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when choosing an item from a drop-down list.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p162">修正此問題：在法文或德文版 Excel 中，透過 INDIRECT 函數使用 R1C1 樣式參考時，沒有產生參考或預期的值，而是造成 \#REF! 錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p162">Fix an issue where using the R1C1-style reference in the INDIRECT function with a French or German version of Excel results in a \#REF! error instead of the referenced and expected value.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-873">修正此問題：在「自訂清單」對話方塊中建立自訂排序清單時，無法使用 ENTER 鍵來分隔清單項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-873">Fix an issue where the ENTER key doesn't work to separate list entries when creating a custom sort list in the Customs Lists dialog box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p163">修正此問題：複製或移動資訊時會出現錯誤訊息，例如「無法開啟剪貼簿」或「我們無法釋放剪貼簿上的空間，可能有另一個程式正在使用它」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p163">Fix an issue where copying or moving information causes an error message to appear, such as "Cannot open the Clipboard" or "We couldn't free up space on the Clipboard. Another program might be using it right now."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-876">修正此問題：嘗試編輯包含許多文字方塊的活頁簿時，Excel 停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-876">Fix an issue where Excel hangs when trying to edit a workbook that contains numerous text boxes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-877">修正由目前安全性更新造成的問題：從不受信任的位置開啟 HTML 檔時，不是允許使用者在受保護的檢視中開啟檔案，而是開啟畫面空白 (沒有內容) 的 Excel，且沒有顯示錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-877">Fix an issue, caused by a recent security update, where opening an HTML file from an untrusted location opens Excel with a blank (empty) screen with no errors displayed, instead of allowing the user to open the file in Protected View.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-878">修正此問題：插入以無效範圍為依據的樞紐分析表時，會顯示不正確的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-878">Fix an issue where inserting a PivotTable based on an invalid range causes an incorrect error message to display.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-879">修正此問題：當您儲存的活頁簿包含使用 Application.OnUndo 的程式設計復原層級時，您對活頁簿所做的最後一次變更會被復原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-879">Fix an issue where when you save a workbook that includes a programmatic undo level by using Application.OnUndo, the last change to the workbook is undone.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-940">商務用 Skype：安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-940">Skype for Business: Security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-941">Microsoft 資訊安全佈告欄 [MS16-097](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/security/ms16-097)：Microsoft 圖形元件的安全性更新 (3177393)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-941">Microsoft Security Bulletin [MS16-097](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/security/ms16-097): Security Update for Microsoft Graphics Component (3177393)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-942">Microsoft 資訊安全佈告欄 [MS16-120](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/security/ms16-120)：Microsoft 圖形元件的安全性更新 (3192884)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-942">Microsoft Security Bulletin [MS16-120](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/security/ms16-120): Security Update for Microsoft Graphics Component (3192884)</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cfde-943">商務用 Skype：非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-943">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-944">修正此問題：在 Window 10 版本 1607 (也稱為「年度更新版」) 上，共用次要監視器的選項沒有在特定監視器設定中出現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-944">Fix an issue where the option to share a secondary monitor doesn't appear with certain monitor configurations on Window 10 Version 1607 (also known as the Anniversary Update).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-945">修正此問題：當共用者使用 RDP 的協力廠商實作並聚焦至共用內容時，商務用 Skype 發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-945">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when zooming into shared content when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p169">修正此問題：當商務用 Skype 透過連接埠 443 與 SIP 伺服器連線，且 Proxy 伺服器已存在時，如果 Proxy 不允許這些連線，則登入程序中會發生嚴重的延遲。透過在 HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync 下新增 EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 登錄項目，並將值設為 1，可啟用修正程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p169">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections. The fix is enabled by adding the EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD registry entry under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync, and setting the value to 1.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-948">修正此問題：在使用者執行 Windows 7 時，首先共用了主要顯示器，接著切換為共用第二個顯示器，而檢視者看到黑色畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-948">Fix an issue where viewers see a black screen when a user is running Windows 7 and shares the main monitor first, and then switches to share a second monitor.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-949">修正此問題：已將使用者移轉至 Exchange Online 之後，使用者無法連線到 Exchange 來取得交談記錄、連絡人或語音信箱資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-949">Fix an issue where the user can't connect to Exchange to get conversation history, contact, or voicemail information after the user has been migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-950">修正此問題：交談視窗嘗試將資訊貼入撥號盤或者白板中的文字註解時，會不正確地將資訊貼入聊天輸入文字方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-950">Fix an issue with the conversation window where trying to paste information into the dial pad or into text annotations in the whiteboard incorrectly pastes the information into the chat input text box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-951">修正此問題：商務用 Skype 在使用不同解析度的監視器 (尤其是高解析度監視器) 時，不會隨著監視器變更更新縮放比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-951">Fix an issue where Skype for Business doesn't update scaling with monitor changes when using monitors with different resolutions, especially high resolution monitors.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-952">修正此問題：使用鍵盤來檢視 IM 轉換中的參與者清單時，鍵盤焦點錯誤地移至聊天記錄，而未顯示參與者清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-952">Fix an issue where, when using the keyboard to view the list of participants in an IM conversion, the keyboard focus incorrectly moves to chat history instead of showing the list of participants.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-953">修正此問題：使用高對比 Windows 佈景主題時，[參與者動作] 畫面上的工具提示消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-953">Fix an issue where the tooltips on the Participant Actions screen disappear when using a high contrast Windows theme.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-954">修正此問題：電話號碼的位置未顯示在會議邀請中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-954">Fix an issue where the location of phone numbers isn't shown in meeting invites.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-955">修正此問題：高 DPI 的遠端控制案例中的滑鼠指標問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-955">Fix an issue with the mouse pointer in remote control scenarios with high DPI.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-956">修正此問題：當其他參與者切換要顯示哪個共用桌面時，參與者看不到共用桌面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-956">Fix an issue where a participant can't see the shared desktop when other participants switch which shared desktop is being displayed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-957">修正此問題：登入因為憑證問題而失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-957">Fix an issue where sign in fails with a certificate issue.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-958">修正此問題：從 [圖庫檢視] 切換到 [內容檢視] 再切換回 [圖庫檢視] 時，未在螢幕頂端載入 [白板檢視]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-958">Fix an issue where the Whiteboard View doesn't load at the top of screen when switching from Gallery View to Content View and back to Gallery View.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-959">修正此問題：在 Exchange 驗證期間登入失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-959">Fix an issue with sign in failures during Exchange authentication.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-960">修正此問題：當共用者使用 RDP 的協力廠商實作且共用者的解析度低於檢視器的解析度時，如果檢視將 Skype 視窗最大化，則商務用 Skype 會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-960">Fix an issue where, when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP and the sharer's resolution is lower than the viewer's resolution, Skype for Business crashes if the view maximizes the Skype window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-961">修正此問題：[內容] 按鈕無法在 [會議室前方] 顯示上運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-961">Fix an issue where the Content button doesn't work on the Front of Room display.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-962">修正此問題：如果電腦已設定為將 Internet Explorer 中的內部 Proxy pac 檔案 URL 當作自動組態指令碼，則無法在該電腦上重新加入會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-962">Fix an issuer where rejoining a meeting fails on computers configured for internal proxy pac file URLs in Internet Explorer as an automatic configuration script.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-963">修正此問題：使用鍵盤快速鍵將影片設為靜音或關閉影片時，螢幕助讀程式 (例如 [朗讀程式]) 未宣告所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-963">Fix an issue where, when using keyboard shortcuts to mute or turn off a video, screen readers, such as Narrator, don't announce the changes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-964">修正此問題：[編輯位置] 對話方塊沒有螢幕助讀程式 (例如 [朗讀程式]) 可以使用的標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-964">Fix an issue where the Edit Location dialog box didn't have labels that screen readers, such as Narrator, could use.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-965">修正此問題：螢幕助讀程式 (例如 [朗讀程式]) 未正確地處理功能區下方顯示的警示通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-965">Fix an issue where screen readers, such as Narrator, don't correctly handle the alert notifications that appear just under the ribbon.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-966">修正此問題：端對端的視訊型螢幕共享工作階段會造成 CPU 使用量增加，以及在簡報者使用一個或多個超高畫質 (ultra-high-definition) 顯示器時，造成簡報者電腦上的應用程式和作業系統回應變差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-966">Fix an issue where a peer-to-peer video-based screen-sharing session causes increased CPU usage and makes apps and the operating system less responsive on the presenter's computer if the presenter is using one or more ultra-high-definition displays.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-967">修正此問題：將商務用 Skype 視窗重新調整至最小高度時，會造成語音郵件清單無法顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-967">Fix an issue where resizing the Skype for Business window to the minimum height causes the voice mail list to not be visible.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-968">修正此問題：在開啟或建立 Skype 會議後，按一下 [會議選項] 按鈕會造成 Outlook 當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-968">Fix an issue where clicking on Meeting Options button after opening or creating a Skype meeting causes Outlook to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-969">修正此問題：儲存的聊天記錄在 Outlook 中顯示為草稿郵件訊息，且無法加以回覆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-969">Fix an issue where a saved chat history appeared in Outlook as a draft mail message and couldn't be replied to.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-970">修正此問題：如果使用者變更 Office 中的預設語言，主視窗標題的語言並不會變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-970">Fix an issue where the language of the main window title doesn't change if the user changes the default language in Office.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-971">修正此問題：[關係] 索引標籤會多次顯示外部連絡人，而非僅顯示一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-971">Fix an issue where the Relationship tab shows an external contact multiple times instead of just once.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-972">修正此問題：當收件者無法收到離線訊息時，使用者看到錯誤的「僅限離線訊息」訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-972">Fix an issue where user incorrectly sees "Offline messages only" message when recipient can't receive offline messages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-973">修正此問題：使用者在 Exchange Server 新增委派後，委派未顯示在商務用 Skype 中，即使重新啟動電腦也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-973">Fix an issue where after a user adds a delegate in Exchange Server, the delegate doesn't show up in Skype for Business even after restarting it.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-974">修正此問題：設定重新開啟交談的選項後，索引標籤會在登入時消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-974">Fix an issue where tabs disappear when signing in when the option to reopen conversations is set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-975">修正此問題：螢幕助讀程式無法在新訊息送達 IM 交談時宣告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-975">Fix an issue where a screen reader can't announce when a new message arrives in an IM conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-976">修正螢幕助讀程式的鍵盤瀏覽和朗讀文字相關問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-976">Fix issues with keyboard navigation and narrated text for a screen reader.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-977">修正此問題：螢幕助讀程式未宣告畫面共享已啟動且使用者可以看到此畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-977">Fix an issue where a screen reader doesn't announce that screen sharing has started and that people can see the screen.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-978">修正此問題：當使用者使用與會議主持組織不同盟的帳戶加入會議時，使用者會看到空白交談視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-978">Fix an issue where the user sees a blank conversation window when the user joins a meeting using an account that's not federated with the organization hosting the meeting.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p171">**在功能區上群組共同作業功能：** 在功能區上，將共用、聊天、註解和文件活動等功能，以及目前正在編輯文件的使用者群組在一起。 [詳細資訊](https://blogs.office.com/2016/04/26/new-to-office-365-in-april-skype-for-business-mac-preview-bringing-collaboration-to-the-forefront-in-office-and-more/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p171">**Collaboration features grouped together on the ribbon:** Features such as Share, Chat, comments, document activity, and who is currently editing the document are grouped together on the ribbon. -   <span data-ttu-id="8cfde-p172">**點選：** 尋找並重複使用您組織的相關文件內容。 [詳細資訊](https://support.office.com/article/860118fc-1f61-41f6-922f-40084a284658)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cfde-p172">**Tap:** Find and reuse content from your organization’s relevant documents.
